---
layout: "post"
title: "Simple Typed Lambda Calculus"
date: "2018-08-17"
categories: type-theory
toc: true
agda: true
latex: true
---

We present a formalisation of the syntax in Agda for the *Simple Typed Lambda
Calculus (STLC)* with some of its properties and the description of the
type-checking for this type system. We refactor the implementation by
[@gergoerdi](https://github.com/gergoerdi/stlc-agda/) for this calculus,
in particular the [Scopecheck](https://github.com/jonaprieto/stlctalk/blob/master/src/Scopecheck.agda)
and [Typecheck](https://github.com/jonaprieto/stlctalk/blob/master/src/Typecheck.agda) module.

The following source code tested with:

- Agda v2.5.4
- Agda Standard Library v0.16

The original content was firstly exposed at EAFIT in Seminar of Logic:

  - [Slides](https://github.com/jonaprieto/stlctalk/raw/master/slides/slides.pdf).
  - Repository: [https://github.com/jonaprieto/stlctalk](https://github.com/jonaprieto/stlctalk).

{: .foldable }

### Bound

Lambda terms using De Bruijn indexes.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="2035" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="Bound"></a><a id="2042" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#2042" class="Module">Bound</a> <a id="2048" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="2049" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#2049" class="Bound">Type</a> <a id="2054" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="2056" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a><a id="2059" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="2061" class="Keyword">where</a>

      <a id="3179" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="3181" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#3099" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="3183" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#2732" class="Datatype Operator">⊢</a> <a id="3185" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#1480" class="InductiveConstructor">lam</a> <a id="3189" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="3190" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#3088" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="3192" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#1400" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">∶</a> <a id="3194" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#3090" class="Bound">A</a><a id="3195" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="3197" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#3092" class="Bound">t</a> <a id="3199" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#2732" class="Datatype Operator">⇝</a> <a id="3201" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#2419" class="InductiveConstructor">lam</a> <a id="3205" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#3090" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="3207" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#3094" class="Bound">t&#39;</a>

### Scopecheck

Check representation of λ-terms using de Bruijn indexes.
Get a λ-term using de Bruijn indexes by given a λ-term with names.

{: .foldable }
<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="4264" class="Comment">-- ∃-syntax and ∄-syntax</a>

    <a id="5886" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="5888" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="5889" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#5889" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="5891" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="5893" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#2589" class="Function">Binder</a> <a id="5900" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#5879" class="Bound">n</a><a id="5901" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="5903" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="5905" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="5906" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#5906" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="5908" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="5910" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#1310" class="Function">Name</a><a id="5914" class="Symbol">)</a>
    <a id="5920" class="Comment">------------------------------</a>
    <a id="5955" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="5957" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Relation.Nullary.html#534" class="Datatype">Dec</a> <a id="5961" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="5962" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#4407" class="Function">∃[</a> <a id="5965" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#5965" class="Bound">t</a> <a id="5967" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#4407" class="Function">]</a> <a id="5969" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="5970" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#5889" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="5972" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#2732" class="Datatype Operator">⊢</a> <a id="5974" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#1456" class="InductiveConstructor">var</a> <a id="5978" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#5906" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="5980" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#2732" class="Datatype Operator">⇝</a> <a id="5982" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#5965" class="Bound">t</a><a id="5983" class="Symbol">))</a>

              <a id="6677" class="Keyword">with</a> <a id="6682" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#5265" class="Function">name-dec</a> <a id="6691" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#6651" class="Bound">Γ,y⊢varx⇝t</a>
            <a id="6714" class="Symbol">...</a>  <a id="6719" class="Symbol">|</a> <a id="6721" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Data.Sum.Base.html#470" class="InductiveConstructor">inj₁</a> <a id="6726" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#6726" class="Bound">x≡y</a>                    <a id="6749" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="6751" class="Bound">x≢y</a> <a id="6755" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#6726" class="Bound">x≡y</a>
            <a id="6771" class="Symbol">...</a>  <a id="6776" class="Symbol">|</a> <a id="6778" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Data.Sum.Base.html#495" class="InductiveConstructor">inj₂</a> <a id="6783" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#6783" class="Bound">p</a><a id="6784" class="Symbol">@(</a><a id="6786" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#6786" class="Bound">t′</a> <a id="6789" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#139" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">-by-</a> <a id="6794" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#6794" class="Bound">Γ⊢varx⇝t′</a><a id="6803" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="6805" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="6807" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#6535" class="Bound">∄t⟨Γ⊢varx⇝t⟩</a> <a id="6820" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#6783" class="Bound">p</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

We want to determine if given a variable context and a term,
it is possible to find its encoding using De Bruijn indexes.
If so, we got its respective construction for that lambda term.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="Scopecheck.check"></a><a id="7036" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#7036" class="Function">check</a>
    <a id="7046" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="7048" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="7050" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="7051" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#7051" class="Bound">n</a><a id="7052" class="Symbol">}</a>
    <a id="7058" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="7060" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7061" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#7061" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="7063" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="7065" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#2589" class="Function">Binder</a> <a id="7072" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#7051" class="Bound">n</a><a id="7073" class="Symbol">)</a>
    <a id="7079" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="7081" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7082" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#7082" class="Bound">t</a> <a id="7084" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="7086" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#1435" class="Datatype">S.Expr</a><a id="7092" class="Symbol">)</a>
    <a id="7098" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="7100" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Relation.Nullary.html#534" class="Datatype">Dec</a> <a id="7104" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7105" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#4407" class="Function">∃[</a> <a id="7108" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#7108" class="Bound">t′</a> <a id="7111" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#4407" class="Function">]</a> <a id="7113" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7114" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#7061" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="7116" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#2732" class="Datatype Operator">⊢</a> <a id="7118" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#7082" class="Bound">t</a> <a id="7120" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#2732" class="Datatype Operator">⇝</a> <a id="7122" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#7108" class="Bound">t′</a><a id="7124" class="Symbol">))</a>

  <a id="7130" class="Comment">-- By induction on the term syntax.</a>

  <a id="8656" class="Comment">-- Go from a representation that uses Names to one that uses de Bruijn indices</a>
  <a id="Scopecheck.scope"></a><a id="8737" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#8737" class="Function">scope</a> <a id="8743" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="8745" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="8746" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#8746" class="Bound">t</a> <a id="8748" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="8750" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#1435" class="Datatype">S.Expr</a><a id="8756" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="8758" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="8760" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="8761" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#8761" class="Bound">p</a> <a id="8763" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="8765" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Relation.Nullary.Decidable.html#897" class="Function">True</a> <a id="8770" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="8771" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#7036" class="Function">check</a> <a id="8777" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Data.Vec.html#712" class="InductiveConstructor">[]</a> <a id="8780" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#8746" class="Bound">t</a><a id="8781" class="Symbol">)}</a> <a id="8784" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="8786" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#2364" class="Datatype">Expr</a> <a id="8791" class="Number">0</a>
  <a id="8795" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#8737" class="Function">scope</a> <a id="8801" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#8801" class="Bound">t</a> <a id="8803" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="8804" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#8804" class="Bound">p</a><a id="8805" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="8807" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="8809" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#155" class="Field">proj₁</a> <a id="8815" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="8816" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Relation.Nullary.Decidable.html#1055" class="Function">toWitness</a> <a id="8826" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#8804" class="Bound">p</a><a id="8827" class="Symbol">)</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

    <a id="10522" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#10458" class="Function">K</a> <a id="10524" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="10526" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#9927" class="InductiveConstructor">tLam</a> <a id="10531" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="10532" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#9927" class="InductiveConstructor">tLam</a> <a id="10537" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#9861" class="InductiveConstructor">tVar</a><a id="10541" class="Symbol">)</a>

    <a id="10548" class="Keyword">postulate</a>
      <a id="Typing.A"></a><a id="10564" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#10564" class="Postulate">A</a> <a id="10566" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="10568" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#9450" class="Datatype">Type</a>
      <a id="Typing.B"></a><a id="10579" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#10579" class="Postulate">B</a> <a id="10581" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="10583" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#9450" class="Datatype">Type</a>
      <a id="Typing.C"></a><a id="10594" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#10594" class="Postulate">C</a> <a id="10596" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="10598" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#9450" class="Datatype">Type</a>

    <a id="10608" class="Comment">-- S : [] ⊢ lam (A ↣ (B ↣ C))</a>
    <a id="10642" class="Comment">--              (lam (A ↣ B)</a>
    <a id="10675" class="Comment">--                   (lam A</a>
    <a id="10707" class="Comment">--                     ((var (# 2)) ∙ (var (# 0))) ∙ ((var (# 1)) ∙ (var (# 0))) ))</a>
    <a id="10795" class="Comment">--        ∶ (A ↣ (B ↣ C)) ↣ (A ↣ B) ↣ A ↣ C</a>
    <a id="10843" class="Comment">-- S = tLam (tLam ((tLam ({! tVar  !} ∙ {!   !})) ∙ ({! tVar  !} ∙ {!   !}))) --  tLam (tLam (tLam ((tVar ∙ tVar) ∙ (tVar ∙ tVar))))</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

### References
